About the job

Contract Developer: Node.js & Terraform – Remote (UK only) - 3 month contract


A CTO‑led, discreet startup is seeking an experienced Node.js backend contractor to build a greenfield API foundation , replacing an outsourced system with an in‑house solution. This is a critical, high‑visibility role, ideal for someone who thrives on autonomy, quality, and clean delivery.


Key Responsibilities

  • Architect and build a new API in Node.js , using NestJS for clear and maintainable backend structure.
  • Design, implement, and manage Infrastructure as Code with Terraform , deploying secure, scalable services to Azure.
  • Ensure ISO‑grade controls and PII handling across deployment and runtime.
  • Drive CI/CD and release processes into production.
  • Direct stakeholder meetings with the CTO on a day to day basis


What We’re Looking For

  • 5+ years in Node.js backend development (NestJS preferred).
  • Proven Terraform usage on Azure or AWS.
  • Strong understanding of security, compliance (ISO 27001) , and PII protection.
  • Near‑native spoken and written English.
  • Experience with PSC contracting and IR35 .


Interview Process (Designed to Be Fast & Fair)

  • Initial 30‑min call – behavioural & approach‑oriented, no coding.
  • Final 30‑min call – scenario review, follow‑up questions, and clarifying priorities, leading to an offer.

About the company

Corecom Consulting
114,360 followers
IT Services and IT Consulting 11-50 employees 49 on LinkedIn

Corecom Consulting is The UK’s Leading IT Recruitment Company headquartered in Leeds, with a European division. We offer permanent and contract IT recruitment services and have successfully delivered large recruitment campaigns for some of the UK’s best-known brands – from tech start-ups right through to FTSE listed organisations.

We pride ourselves on our innovative, digital candidate attraction strategies and offer bespoke employer brand solutions ensuring our clients are at the front of the queue for the best tech talent in an increasingly competitive market.
Our clients enjoy our refreshing and honest approach. They choose to partner with Corecom Consulting to utilise our brand and reach within the technology community, our innovative candidate attraction methods, bespoke employer brand services and excellent delivery record.

As a multi-award winning IT recruitment company, we are passionate about our candidates and passionate about social change. That’s why we do things a little differently to others. We listen, advocate and work in tandem with our candidates and clients to find the right cultural, skill and development fit to ensure success and longevity in the next step of your career. Our commitment to autonomy, development and wellbeing ensures unfaltering exceptional client service and a very happy team.

We host monthly award-winning networking events designed to add real, demonstrable value to managers across the full IT spectrum. Our Boss Events Series provides you with ‘the board you can’t afford’ and allows IT managers to come together in a unique environment to share their experiences, whilst learning from reputable and established speakers who are leaders in the industry.

To find out more visit our website and get in touch: http://www.corecomconsulting.co.uk …
